THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
[See Rule 7]
FORM OF NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION(1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF 
LANDS FOR INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997 
(CLA-SIP/2024/34/12/04/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(c-1)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997(Tamil Nadu 
Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an 
extent of 21.9450 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for SIPCOT - Cheyyar 
Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

No.VI(1)/692(c-4)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
  Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 12.7750 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit, 
Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-SIP/2024/34/10/02/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(c-5)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 21.1950 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Tiruvannamalai may be inspected on any day during office hours.

NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 16.6100 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 23.0650 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-SIP/2024/34/06/01/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(c-8)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 20.3800 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu 
Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 19.9750 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit, Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-SIP/2024/40/08/02/0001)
No.VI(1)/692(c-14)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition 
of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 12.3250 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar(LA), Unit, 
Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
